Of which one way is that you make three cauterizations, or four, lining according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the fire cautery of the liver that we have said before; and do not press your hand on all the cautery, and let the mouse rest on his back; and another way of cautery is that you heat the cautery that has two sides, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and place the scar that is at the place of the mouse, or the cut comes towards the left, and let the elevation that you feel with the scar according to the scar, according to the length of the body, and the cautery be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After you put the two men to bed and they can no longer be heard on the other side, then treat with fire, and so on there will be three. And if you see it, then treat with fire all three.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the cure has gotten worse over a long time, and this is evident before the other one mentioned.
de ydropisie	dropy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Does not suit for dropy, except by the way called "ascleotes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat according to the ways we have spoken of in the divisions, and your cure does not benefit from it, then you must make four cauterizations around the body, one on the belly, one on the liver, one on the kidney, two behind the back along the spine, and one on the penis; and let the cauterizations be close to the skin of the patient.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After let the fire cautery go for to get rid of long and tenous purging, and do not leave the cure of the patient after the cautery; and healing would hurry, and the two intentions will come together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the abdomen is the key that we have in front of us, and according to what it is, it will be olive-shaped.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the pieces
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the pieces are swollen in those who are hydropic and are pale yellow, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the index and the middle finger; and gently lift your hand with the cautery without returning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too far in all cases, otherwise it would force the yellow pus, and do the cauterization according to this shape:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After you have done with the two legs, make two cauterizations in each leg at the tip of the scrotum; and let the cauterization be long, one on the outside of the thigh before, and the other behind it, alongside the leg; and leave the cauterizations in place for a long time without treating them, since they will do so themselves; after you have done this for one leg, then go on to treat the others as we have said.
de la menoison	of the dungeon
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the water in the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the digestive and beneficial virtues that are in the stomach and intestines are afflailed, and cannot be treated by any means of treatment; and you see the sick person suffer greatly and of great virtue, so make a great cauterization on the stomach according to what he has spoken about it before, or a cauterization of the stomach, circulating; and four cauterizations around the navel finely, at every cauterization nailed finely, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then make a fire cautery on his hand, and I make a cautery on each finger, and II small cauteries on the stomach of him who has much, because the cure is profitable when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	for the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhoids are at the foundation, or one or more, and are old and have large cold, damp,腐った腫れ、そしてそれらは私たちが上記の章で言ったように治療されている場合、火の cauteryは役に立たず：I背中の中ほどに cauteryを施し、三角形の形をして少しずつ切り落とし、IIの cauteryを同じように行い、もしあなたが考えて、患者の胃が冷えているなら、肉は煮えず、顔が膨らむことがわかったら、それなら我々は前にも述べたように胃に1つの cauteryを行い、肝臓にIつの cauteryを行い、そしてまた我々が前に言ったように鼠道全体を cauterizeする。そして cauteryを長く開いておきなさい。
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let him rest as long as he is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the flesh which is called "thelol
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat the flesh, if it is heated, put the fire-cauterizer on it and let it burn until it reaches the root of the flesh; then treat with oil that helps until it is healthy; and if you treat with a large cauldron, do so once or twice, and if there is much flesh, cauterize it as we have said; after treating with beneficial oils as long as they are healthy; and if you treat with a large fire-cauterizer on the flesh, it will be more helpful.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound that has been ill-treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear a cut or an opening, which we will describe in our own way, there comes a disease that cannot be cured except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no vent in the fistula, and it wakes up and gets putrid and corrupted moisture, then you should provide an all-encompassing subtle tent, and remember that you know how much it has of perfection.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After warming the cauterizer that seems like a razor, and pouring it into the fistula according to the quantity that the tent has entered, and starting over with the cauterizer until the corrupting and rotten flesh is burned, once or twice, depending on the quantity of what is needed; and be careful of the nerves that are inside, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes into the body of the belly and the intestine, then be careful of these veins, and do not make a cut except in the flesh, and think that it is not useless; after treating the part until it is healthy, and if the veins are broken, and the matter is dried up over a long time, then know that the vein is completely healed; and if the matter is not dried up, know that the vein is three-quarters healed, and the bone is corrupted at its base; and so as one of these that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain of the kidneys and great windiness comes on, and does not take hold of a woman, then it is necessary that you make a cautery on the kidneys from one side to the other at the clavicle cautery which we have before mentioned; and if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizes in a line, and greater help will be done.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is soft and weak from pain and moisture, so that the patient retenes urine, then you make a cautery on the back part of the bladder, where the hair grows on the tip of the penis, and one on each side, and each so long as an inch; and you make another cautery behind, where you need it; and you make the cauterizes clavicular according to the form before mentioned.
de la marris	from the mare
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the mare is cold and damp, and does not allow it to conceive, and the flowers are corrupted and late in blooming; and when they do come, then there is great pain: therefore it is necessary that you make three cauters around the udder, as we have said above in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauters on the back; and let the cauters be heated, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the haunch
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip joint pocket, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the joints are found to be hot, then you must cauterize the patient on the hip joint pocket with a circle-like cauterizing iron, and mark in front of the joint inside the circle as it moves back; and if so, let the cauterization be such as that which we have described for the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you do not have the fire cautery, then make III cauteries from the large olive oil, and let the cauterization be perfect as all the courses; and treat until he is well.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When the pain comes in the box of the hip, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then you must purges the patient of the large humors with foul pills, or other bad-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After that you make the cautery; and the method of the cautery is according to two methods: that is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery is according to many methods, some of which are: you make three triangular cauterizations according to this form, and you make them deep and large, and there is between each cauterization the thickness of two fingers, and let the cauterizations be olive oil; never do a cauterization in the middle on the top of the hip, for there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, whether the fire cautery at the circle that we have said before in the dislocation of the hip; but do it in a different way that the circles contain all the hip, and all the skin of the cure is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way that is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip, and does not reach up to the thigh or up to the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the pain comes up to the thigh and leg, then do II fire cauteries at the place where the patient says that the pain is, and one cautery above the ankle three times on the left side; and let the cauterization be scalded, and let the skin of the cure be burned; and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two or three toes or near the ankle, then cauterize at the point where the pain is III or IV times with the fire cautery called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	Et si tu veux être un bon guérisseur, fais-le avec soin; et s'il souffre d'une douleur à l'intérieur du genou qui irradie vers la cuisse, applique un cautère à l'aide d'un couteau ou d'une pince, et prends bien garde à tous tes cautères pour ne pas en laisser échapper un qui brûlerait les nerfs et les grandes artères, et ne causerais ainsi au patient une souffrance et une contraction importantes.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen many who made a cauterization on the foot's arch, letting it go so long that the leg was completely twisted, and the toes too, and became pierced and腐腐したすべての toe.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	Après une solution abdominale dont il est mort.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	Et si le douleur est en deux parties ensemble, fais un cautère dans chacune d'elles, selon cette manière.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	Et le sage dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l'un entrechetres jusc'a l'autre d'espaice la quantiteit d'un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c'est li forme:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the sages said in the cauterization of the hinch, since this is the way, make it such a bar and be at the top as well as thick as a nail, or a little less, and be between chetresses and be from one chetresse to another of space the quantity of a nut; and let the chetresses come above from both sides, and also be like nails, and I have a lot of good made iron; and this is the form:
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says that we use little of this cautery because of the fear of its heat, and few who use it; but this is a good cautery which can bear it, and leave it where it afflicts.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The medicine cautery that burns well, make a tool with an opening at the edge of the door, and it is either made of brass or iron to one side, and in height it has two of us, and each of them is wide to this quantity of the thickness of two fingers; and may be opened up and down, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting on the bag over the hip of the lying-down patient on his side, and pressing your hand well up against the bag; after pouring in between the two circles of hot water that has been heated by the fire a little while, and leaving it for an hour, allow the pain and burning sensation to the patient.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain extends only to the thigh or only to the leg, then you make the instrument smaller according to what you have done in the hip joint plus; and this is the way of hot wax, and I wrote it and treated it for the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline and live charcoal, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together, and put them into a nine-part pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Or take a small space somewhere that the point of one scalpel can enter; and put that pot on top of another well-lined pot, and put alkaline and charcoal and warm wax on it, as much as you need to cover the two powders when you shake them up in your hand; and let it be like that until it has dried out a little water and wood, then take all that wax, and spread it over the charcoal and over the alkali just as it was before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And then if it is moist and amenable to the work of medicine and other cauteries Because she does this operation like fire, and with other medicines which cauterize well the knee here as thyme and honey of the acorn tree and calce with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galileo tells us of a cure in which an honourable man was cured of the pain in his knee and sciatica, and he was very wet, and said that no other cure was made, and that he was cured at one go when this cure was made, and he bathed himself as it is taught here after.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And he said in this way that you grind the green lime very fine and dry, and mix it with a little fat, and put it on the knee and thigh and leg where the pain is, and let it rest; and let him be for three hours, and by the quantity so that the patient no longer feels the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then put him into a bath as long as his body is a little awake, and let him lie in the water, and the pain will all go away and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use fire cautery with these medicines, unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Diascorides says that when the sciatic vein is burned with the end of a goat's horn, it helps much; and the cautery must be done in some such way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take another and rub it with old oil, and put it on the pit that is between the thumb of the hand and the other that is called the palm.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After take a piece of dried goat's horn, and hold it in the fire until it is full of charcoal, and put it on the wool, and leave it until it stops hurting; and then do it again, and never stop doing it as long as you think that it comes up to the knee, and that the pain has stopped; and this way of cauterizing is called "goat's horn cautery.
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of two
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, or from sitting down or from impact, or from excessive evacuation, or from the appearance of expanded cold matter, no one of these appearances is worth the cauterization, unless it comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary that after this, the patient is voided of foul pills or other appearances, that a line is made on the back at the place where the pain is, three lines with an inch apart, and in each line V cauterizations or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure; and let the cauterization be done according to the cauterization that is called 'point'; and if you see, do III cauterizations or IV at the clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often occurs in small children, and the signs of its onset are that they become constricted when they stand up, and they are afraid; and you find in the last spine at the back, and in us there is an appearance that comes on the others.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this person and you want to cure him, cauterize him with fire according to this method.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	Burn each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see this, burn inside the spine with a sharp fire that is two or three lines long, and let the burns be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Afterwards, cure the area until it is healthy according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply fire to gangrene which is in the spine of the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When there is pain in the joints due to moisture that spreads to each limb, and when pain comes in pieces, what is called "podagra" properly, and when it is of a cold cause and cannot be cured with medicines, then it is cured with fire in this way: Make the fire cauterization around the joint of the foot, and let the fire be olive-colored according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary that you touch the face of the foot, then make a fire cautery to all the fire cauteries that are claimed "zero".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains come only to the genitals and other joints, and this happens many times, then make a fire cautery on each kneecap three cauteries or four of each part, at all the olive cauterization; and if you need more, do so, but do not hold your hand too long except when the skin of the heel is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend only to the knees and back, then administer the cautery that we have spoken about in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, then do not enter more than two lines; and if there is still pain in the two joints and the hair of the hand; and if the pains come only to the wrist or only to the shoulders, then cauterize each part, and well govern the patient and apply medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you do this well and you purge the phlegm, you will be healed by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	for the cut of the surgeon
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the cut has come to a halt and the bleeding has stopped, and you have healed him with your hand, let him not move that day; and he should use things that cool his belly, so that the end [of the cut] drops from his belly; then he shall sit down upon his back between your hands, and command him to wet his hair as long as the cuts are healing, and bring them to your two hands, and sign of one side of the cut upon the bone of the finger, and at all a form like half a circle overhead; then heat the fire of which is this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and drops slowly.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then return the balls to their place; and let the minister dry his hand so that it does not turn back; and work well on the legs of the patient, and put a towel on him and an iron on his legs, and another on his feet which dry his hands; then set the cauterizer on his bone with your whole hand, and hold it straight and as long as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, try again another time until you come to the bone; and be careful that the ball does not slip when you make the cauterization; so you do not burn it; and that by this the patient does not die, or any other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you come to the bone with the cauterizer, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that the cauterizer of children be subtle according to their measure, and of grown-ups too great according to their measure; after III days cure the place of the cauterizer of butter until the heat subsides; after the cure of other medicines until he is well, and let the patient lie on his back for XX days until the wound is well sealed; and it is necessary that his bandages be kept on for a long time, so that the ball does not slip when he gets up to go to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, a well-made strap is provided for him and it is carried for another 40 days; and let there be good rest, that he works little and guards against too much drinking and eating, and too much loud speaking; and when he does this instruction, he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after the cure of his shoulder in his paint.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture from the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When the ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, make a cautery of the cautery according to its quantity, and burn the third part of the cure; after the cure according to what we have said; and none of the ancient ones say that it must be cauterized at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the place of the incision and make a line across the width of the rupture, and another on either side, and all your hand holds fast to all the cauterized spots.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from ancient pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any member, or from a bruise or a wound, and this pain lasts a long time, and medicine does not help it, then it is necessary that it be cauterized at the fire that is called "poins", and be the cauterization according to the length of the member and its smallness and its feebleness and its virtue and its location from torments and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If he is well after the first cauterization, it is good; but if not, then you must apply another cauterization to that one, for it is necessary that he be well who is nearby; so you must apply the cauterizations until the patient is well.
de meselerie	of slumber
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The mesail are helped by cauterization with great help, and least of all does the disease come from the putrefaction of flux and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s'ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l'autre vers lou front a la fin des chevois; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haitrel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc'a l'os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s'en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu'il est devant.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	Now, see to it that the patient lets the hair grow long and even; and if they itch, apply heat to relieve the itch, but do not scratch too much for fear of causing injury. For in this chapter we will speak about how to treat many diseases with fire cauterization: at the beginning of an illness, how to use it to cure a person, and how to avoid causing pain and damage; and how to apply cauterization to different parts of the body, including the head, neck, back, shoulders, arms, legs, hands, feet, and joints. And be careful not to apply fire cauterization to certain bones or organs, or too much heat may cause injury; and do not scratch too much for fear of causing pain.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the more I make a fire cautery, the more aid I give, and profit from it; and know that the patient does not feel pain at the cauterization as the healthy do, because his body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the fire cautery be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	Afterwards, cure the face with flour mixed with honey and other cures until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the swelling comes in any member and is cured with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it is not healthy, then make a fire cautery on the member according to its size; and let the cauterization be only a little bit inside the curve of the cure; then heal it with ointments until it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never does one make cauterization by the hand and at the foot and at the back, to the exit of a nerve that silences the limb, and thus if it is bone, it swells; and however, no one gets in there if he does not know the limbs and the exits of the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	I am unable to translate this line as the text seems to be incomplete or corrupted. Please provide more context or the full text to ensure an accurate translation.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" has come on, and the medicine's power is lost, then cauterize with a perfect fire according to the quantity of the spittle of the cure, until the blenchour is healed, and its color changes; then treat it with flour of rice and lentils, mixed with oil of roses and leaves of plantain, and hawthorn, and each part has a portion; and all are mixed together, bound with a bandage, and applied to the affected area until it is cured.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The cure for leprosy through fire cautery.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the leprosy begins to appear, and you see it stopping, if the cautery is done with fire that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the leprosy.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And yet another says that one should also make the cautery in the middle of the leprosy; and yet another does not seem right to me, for I am afraid that it will become ulcers and rotten, and I have never seen this done; and yet a more correct thing is that it be cauterized all around, with the fire that is called "a circle," as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the poison that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When some have a disease called "adubelati," and it takes long to die or because of the wastefulness of the disease or because the person is too old and has little blood, or because of age; then let them die quickly: then cauterize them all around with small cauterizations by poking; then let it be like that.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	Because she is hurrying towards death.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see her pierced at all the fire, so hot is the fire of which this form is made:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called 'adubelati' as long as the fire has pierced the course, and make such fires that the patient feels the heat in some way so that the course of decay is recognized.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, as long as he is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure by fire with iron:
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another form of disease called 'corrodens', which is nothing other than a swelling of the member, for it swells the members as much as the fire dries up the wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in its early stages that can be cured by fire together with nails, then heat the small and large nails according to what is appropriate for the place where the disease is; after being cauterized on all sides until all corruption has disappeared, and nothing remains of it, so that whatever is corrupted is taken away.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave him for three days, and put on the burned areas oil to suffer with pain until the burns from the fire are healed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the cure of medicines causing blindness.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days the blind cure does not come, it is good; and if not, then begin again the cauterization on that which is delayed corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this medicine is never once cured of the disease by means of fire cauterization; but nevertheless, fire cauterization is of greater help, and I have already said that the cure of the medicine causing blindness is done by division: take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of onions that come to the tip
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	And sometimes happens that at their tips by defuses arises a disease which is called "clos" according to our intention, and it is a big hairy thing which bleeds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterization of this disease is as follows from two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to be known that there are two kinds of cauterization: fire cauterization and water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is this: take a hot iron, like a pen of a vulture, and make it so that it can stick to the nail from all sides, and have thin edges; then put it on hot the nail, and wrap your hand around the nail completely until it comes off at the root; and he makes a plaster of wild mallows crushed with water, and leaves the plaster on for all night, and the nail will come out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with caraway as soon as possible until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by defuses the heart, and many times come to their hands and feet, so it is necessary that you bring the fire cautery of hot water; and it is in this way: take a twig of oak or iron, or a feather of swan, and put it on the nail and the arthrotic joint, that is to say porpuls verrues; and put the twig on so that it purple all around, then put a little hot water on it, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the twig comes to the root of the nail, and can find the hot water path deep until the root; and allow the patient a little of the biting of hot water for an hour; then leave it, and it will be pulled out all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Make another, until you have drained all those who are within, then treat those who cause harm with garlic.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When someone shakes from cold or fever or another thing, it is necessary that you make four or five cauterizations on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each spine; and one cauterization on the feet, and one above the stomach with olive oil cauterization; this will stop the shaking, and quickly heal the person from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled blisters
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	There is one time when visible pustules appear on the body, which come from corruption of large masses of matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is the first time that they appear, then a cauterization should be made on each head of the pustule: a thin cauterization with a branch of miraballe, which is grasped at the fire, or with a root of amara-root that has been slowly ground;
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And in no way are the fire cauterizations applied at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow hair forward from it, but the superfluity which comes from it is broken, and they are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Sometimes there is great pain from the artery that is cut off at the wound which comes to the surface, or when incising an abscess, or when cauterizing a limb, and similar things; and it is a horrible thing to stink up.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And in any case, when there is one, then you hurry to place your index finger on the vein wound, and strain it as much as the blood stops from your index, and no more drops; then you take fire with olive oil, small and large, as many as it is red; then take I, or a large or small according to the wound and its position, and hold the cauterizer on that vein where you are holding your finger, and keep the cauterizer on until the blood stops flowing.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if he burns too much when you feel your pain on the vein, and the cauterization is over, if you take another of the cauterizations that are in the fire quickly.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing one after the other as long as the pain is gone; and be careful that you don't burn the nerve that hurts, and that no other evil comes upon the sick person; and know that when the artery is cut short of [the body part], it cannot be well healed even if it were by one of the four ways we have mentioned: or by cauterization, or by extraction before it is treated, or by a strong thread, or by medicines put on it which have the power to heal blood; and let it be bound and stretched well.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the healing of a tightly bound bandage or burning things placed on it, or similar things, if it does not benefit, do not use it.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and he doesn't have mirable medicine ready, then he must put his two fingers on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch well until it is satisfied above the wound and above the vein; and do not move the skin, but wet it with cold water often so that it is cold all over and thickens and satisfies; and make incisions in front of those to whom cauterization and medicine are needed.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of remedies for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter all diseases for which it is necessary to use fire cautery, or burning medicine, and the methods and causes and instruments and shapes of the cauterizations; and I put this ointment on the back of the head up to the hairline, and I will go into this chapter by that middle way for those who have a headache.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, as I begin to tell you, it is necessary, o man, that you know that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first chapter of cautery, and therefore greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you do not venture into folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For in the ways of men come to cure.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	If it comes from those who have so affected themselves with their disease that they die easily because of the foolishness they practice with their disease, and of the great nature of their illness; then we must fear them.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And of these who give you their meaning, and say: "Wait, I am hungry"; and the disease is pitiable.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not fitting that you grant consent to those who come to you having this mannerism, but show more great courtesy in your honor than in your covetousness, and do not open widely but carefully from him of whom you are certain, and of whom you could have taken and lost; and use prophecy and indication in the treatment of your sick so that health may be converted; and he who will help you to good reputation, and glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords give you good understanding and justice, and if you will ask for the holy inspiration of His hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered you this chapter in explaining by chapters, according to that which is before or the chapter of the cauterizes, which I have devised from the top down, so that you may find more easily that which you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Dou chief plein d’aigue
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	It is known that this disease often occurs in infants and when the baby cries too much, the head of the child is twisted; and it is never answered by this cause that one does not know.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I never saw this disease except in children, and all those that I have seen it come upon quickly die; and by what seems to me it is better to relax the treatment in such cures.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw a child whose shoulders were plain with moisture and the head got heavier every day until it could not be supported; and he believed so much in the moisture that he died, and this moisture is so gathered around the joints on the back, between the curve of the spine and the bones; and the treatment is so hard for him that he gets a big wound at the top of the head; and so far as we know:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper and the abscess larger, then make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If the moisture has broken the bone, and the signs you see are the pits of the head overshooting each side, and the water shoots out strongly when you press it with your hand, and it does not close again: then you should make three incisions in this way around the head:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After you have stripped the bandages and powders, put wine and oil on it, and leave it for five days; then unbind it, and cure the wound with poultices and ointments, and let the head dry out evenly, and give the patient dry meat to eat until the limb is healed and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way to incise is that you look at the opening of the anus, and the assembly of the sharp edge; for it is never in front; it is never behind; it is never on the right; nor is it ever on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	So cut where the anus opens, and the sharpening of the blade, and do according to what you have the power; and beware that you do not block the artery; and come fluttering with blood, so that the patient dies from a burst artery and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of remedy
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When there is a disease that is called "cataract" in the eye or the ear, and the illness is old, and the remedy of medicine does not benefit, then the following remedy is to use cauterization with what one will cover the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	He therefore, since you have covered the eyes, must make the patient stand with his head back; then rub his neck with a sharp towel until the arteries appear, and then strip him of his collar to all the towel; then see where the vein bites, and its lines are after the ears, and they are not closed; then sign the lines of the cheek, then cover both with a spikelet sharp on two sides, until the saw comes out against the bone, and this either through the large of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, cut the spikelet off the artery and cover it above, sawing also as two sides a two.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	When the vein is covered, let it keep jumping upwards continuously.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery does not open on feeling, then you must measure the quantity of the space of three hands, then sign the cheeks and saw to the bone; and what it comes to put forward so is six inches, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the re-expansion of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains on the bone no hole, if the apostemes cut not there, then extract the wound and bind it, and the cure of ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of gristly meat
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the gristly meat of an old person comes, and the catarrh is acquired, due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples and old sore forsened and similar things, and it is medicated by the methods of medical treatments and all that does not benefit him, then we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have told.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is that the patient makes his hair grow again in his temples, and hears the artery opening in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is not too tight but in some men who are too cold; and if it is tightened, then the patient pulls his collar from some sheets, then he rubs the place with any sharp cloth, and raises the place with hot water until the artery appears clearly; then take the spatumile where this form is.
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And then peel the skin lightly until you reach the artery, and then turn it upside down as pincers, and remove all the thin layers that are attached to each part; and if the artery is thin, then turn it into the tip of the hook, and cut off that part according to the quantity of II shoulders.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut off, then there will be no saving for anyone in all things.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And trim the blood of VI c/ down to III; and if the artery is large, then it is necessary that you tie it with II strong double threads of silk, so that it does not come out in front of the wound's bleeding, and comes off from the blood; then cut off what is between the II threads at that same time, and then, if you see, then cauterize the wound with the fire cautery down to the bone as long as the shoulders are cut; and this is the operation of the muedre, if the patient does not have a fever and has a hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the fire cautery is an aid to end the moisture: for this is a more powerful aid against moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	For in the extraction of arteries, it is necessary to fill the place with fine cotton and place a well-made cloth on top; and when you remove them, let medicines made from dry things that produce blood, and tents, until they are well; and if without cutting the artery as much as you can, if you hurry, cover it with cautery, or employ the place of vitriol and extract it with your hand so that the blood is stopped; and if you do not have this [vitriol], put it on the place of cold water until the blood stops, and remove it as it should be; and that which is stiffened and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein on either side with a sharp cautery, but let the cutting be well spaced to keep the heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too soft, then it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus; et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it should have between the two knives one inch of space, and then when you have sown in two places, and you place on fire so that it comes to the bone, and cut the vein in two places; and are kept apart between the two shoulders because this cauldron is not sold from all over; and this is the shape of the cauldron:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the tears of the eyes come down from the veins that are on the forehead of the head of fire, and there is no benefit from the medicine that one does, and you see the face of the sick person turn gray, and feel cold; and if the oil is soft and moist so that the hair of the papers falls off, and the papers are burnt, and scorched by the heat of the tears, then it is necessary to do this cure.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	Et let them call the ancient "cure for contusions", and that is what you do to the patient who has this disease in his or her hair or forehead; then make three cuts evenly along the length of the forehead; and one of these cuts should be like II pairs all together, cutting through the forehead from above downward until it reaches the nose, and the others II pairs by the sides of the bones, and take care not to cut the arteries which are on the sides of the bones; and keep your hand away from the joint of the two jaws, and let each wound have the quantity of III pairs joined together; and have ready a piece of sponge and lots of rags for wiping away the blood, then pour the sputum from II parts since this is the shape:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	And from the incision that is to be made on the temple until the second incision; and peel off all the curse that is between the two cuts up to the bone, and then do the same thing from the middle cut until the other second one, and then remove this sputum forcefully:
